 chennai se kareeb 90 kilometre dur yahaan ke satish dhawan antariksh centre se pieselvi (polar satellite launch whical) ke jariye 1858 kilogram vajani desh ke pehle ‘microwave remote sencing’ upgrah ko 71 ghante tak chali ulti ginati ke baad subah kareeb paanch bajkar 47 minute par prakshepan ke lagbhag 19 minute baad kaksha main sthapit kar diya gaya
 The launch vehicle 'PSLV' of the Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO) has once again established its credibility by completing 20 successful flights with the launch of RISAT-1
 iske dwaara prakshepit kiya gaya yah ab tak sabase baari upgrah he

 isane bharat ke pehle radar imaging satellite ko sateek rup se vaanchit kaksha main sthapit kar diya

 The impact of the "beti Bachao Beti Padhao" campaign has started appearing in Uttar Pradesh
 puure pradesh main prati hajaar beton par 5 betiyon main ijapha hua he, haalanki ab bhi yah aankada chintajanak bana hua he
 In Uttar Pradesh, 906 daughters were born per thousand sons in 2016-17, which has increased to 911 in 2017-18 this year
 yah baat sarkaar ke matra swasthya evam shishu yojana ke survey main saamne ai he
 Somewhere, the effect of "beti Bachao Beti Padhao" is ineffective, somewhere the effect of Prime Minister Modi's campaign, save Beti Padhao, the effect is looking good in UP and it is still inoperable
 lakhanu main bete betiyon kii janm dar ke ausat main hua sudhaar to kanpur, aligarh or mujffarnagar main halaat badtar hue hai
 This year in Lucknow, the birth rate of 11 daughters per thousand has increased
 2016-17 main prati hajaar beton par 892 betiyaan hui thim, jo is saal badhkar 903 ho gai he
 Not only Lucknow, 5 daughters per thousand have increased in the entire state, which gives hope for a good future
 lakhanu ke alaava mau, mainpuri, bijanour, unnav or balrampur main bhi prati hajaar ladakiyon kii sankhya main ijapha hua he
 Many districts are still in bad shape
 raibareli, faijabad, gajiabad, chitrakoot, hapur samet takreeban 27 jile aise hai jahaan prati hajaar ladakiyon kii sankhya ghati he
 In 2016, more than 36 lakh 62 thousand children were born in Uttar Pradesh
 jisamen se 19 lakh, 21 hajaar se zyada ladke the or 17 lakh 41 hajaar se zyada ladkiyaan, lekinis saal ab tak35 lakh se zyada bacchon kaa janm ho chukaa he
 There are more than 18 lakh 69 thousand boys and more than 17 lakh 3 thousand girls
 lakhanu main prati hajaar betiyon ke janm dar main maamuli sudhaar hua he to vahiin aligarh or kanpur main baari kami darj kii gai he
 People living within a radius of 10 km are taking shelter from their relatives and other people through different means
 yuddh kii aahat ko dekhte hue logon ke bich dar kaa maahaul he

"

 vah aazaadee ke pehle desh main sabase budhimaan vakeelon main se ek the

 jaane- motilal nehru ke jivan ke bare main
 
 
 
 - motilal nehru kaa janm 6 may 1861 ko hua tha

 baad main is bhawan ko indira gandhi ne bhartiya sarkaar ko saunp diya tha, jisamen sangrahalay kholaa gaya

 - 1920 main kalakatta ke special congress ke dauraan wo pehali pankti ke netaa the, jinhone asahyog andolan ko apana samarthan diya tha

 '' Piles means piles
 ye kaaphi takalif dene vaali beemaari he
 There is pain in the piles, but this disease also makes it uncomfortable
 piles main swelling ke saath hi tej dard bhi hota he
 According to one study, 50 percent of people get this complaint after crossing the age of 50
 piles se judi sabase badi dikkat ye he ki log iske bare main doctor se baat karne main jhijakte hai or ise chhipate hai
 This disease often increases with the appearance of eavesdropping and increases the risk of infection
 shuruyaat main sirf dard or jalankaa hi ehsaas hota he lekin agar samasya bad jaae to khun aane lagata he
 In the piles, the blood vessels of the anal or rectal area become large, due to which pain occurs with burning sensation
 piles hone ke kai kaaran ho sakate hai
 Sometimes constipation occurs due to poor digestion, lifting heavy things, gas problems, stress, obesity and anal sex
 piles kaa dard har kisi ke liye ek jaisaa ho, ye jaruri nahin
 Pain, itching and burning, swelling and infection in the rectal area are common symptoms
 piles kaa ilaaj sambhav he lekin log jhijak main ilaaj se bachate hai par aap chahen to gharelu upayon kii madad se ise thik kar sakate hai
 You may not believe it, but there is such a thing in your kitchen that you can use it to treat piles within 24 hours
 apple sidar venegar kii madad se aap piles kaa ilaaj kar sakate hai
 How to use it? Apple cider venezar has the property of not allowing infection to increase
 iske istemaal se rectal aria main infections badhane nahin paata he or ye dard kam karne main bhi madad karata he
 Apart from this, it also provides relief in burning sensation
 swelling kam hoti he or aaraam miltaa he
 You can also add aloe vera if you want
 istemaal kaa tarika:1
 Take two spoons of apple cider vinegar in a clean bowl
 2
 Dip a clean piece of cotton wool in it
 3
 Apply this cotton to the affected area
 4
 Do this process until you feel relief

 The smoke spread by burning crop stub (residue roots) and cow dung has made the situation worse in the state
 logon ko saans lene main dikkat mahasoos ho rahi he
 According to the meteorological department, air pollution increases during the winter and mist in the atmosphere remains frozen for a long time
 thand ke dinon main jab taapmaana saamaanya se kam hota he to hawa main tairte maheen dhul kan jam se jate hai
 The government has instructed to stop the work of air pollution-causing stone crusher and multi-storey under-construction buildings for two days
 saath hi yah sunishchit karne ko bhi kaha gaya he ki kisi bhi sthaan par kooda na jalaayaa jaae
 Taking serious note of the haze in the capital city including Lucknow, Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav has directed the Uttar Pradesh Pollution Control Board and the Environment Department to find out the reasons responsible for this mist and take remedial measures
 tippaniyan The Chief Minister said that proper disposal of garbage should be made and to avoid burning it
 yah bhi sunishchit kiya jaae ki vaahan tathaa jenerator pradooshan ke nirdhaarit maanakon ke bheetar chalem

 pradesh main jagah-jagah fasal ke thunth (avshesh jaden) or gobar jalaane se faile dhuen ne sthiti or kharaab kar di he

 mausam vibhaag ke mutabik sheetkaal main hawa nahin chalane se vaayu pradooshan bad jaataa he or vaataavaran main dhundh lambey samay tak jami rahati he

 The survivors of Monday's terrorist attack on the police academy in the Pakistani city of Quetta recalled the horrifying moments between the shootings and the explosions that terrorists used to shoot whoever they saw, and police cadets to escape them
 They were running from windows and roofs by jumping
 balochistan kii rajdhani queta se sate ilaake main bane police training college par somvaar der raat chaar ghante tak jari rahe hamale kii zimmedaari do alag-alag guton ne lee he, jinamein se ek taliban se alag hua aatankwaadi gut he, or doosraa iesas se judaa he
 a spokesman for the paramilitary force Frontier Corps Vasay Khan said that most of the 123 injured and killed were cadets and soldiers
 hamalaa karne aae teen main se do aatankwaadiyon ne khud ko uda liya tha, jabaki teesraa sena kii golibari main dher ho gaya

 mangalvaar ko tivi channelon par bhi queta main hue hamale ke baad academy ke footage dikhaai gai, jisamen jali hui khidkiyaan, or maare gaye or ghayal logon ke juuton se ata padaa farsh dikh rahaa tha

 france se ai media kii khabaron ke anusaar dastavej disienes ke ek purv karmchaaree ne churaae, vahiin bharat ko is bare main kuch bhi likhit main nahin mila he
 More than 22,000 pages of highly confidential information related to the capabilities of the six state-of-the-art submarines released to the Indian Navy in partnership with a French company in Mumbai were leaked, leading to security concerns
 majgaanv godi main francisi pot nirmaataa company disienes dwaara 3
 Information related to the combat capability of the Scorpene submarines being built at a cost of $ 5 billion became public when the Australian newspaper put it on its website
 jab raksha mantri se poocha gaya ki kya disienes ko li ke bare main bharat ko suchit nahin karnaa chahie tha, jo 2011 main hone kii baat kahi ja rahi he to parrikar ne kaha ki sarkaar company se aadhikarik jawaab kaa intjaar karegi
 The comments unhone kaha, 'ek pahalu suraksha kaa he jo hamaare liye pehali praathamikta he
 We have formed a team
 ve li hone kii baat maanakar byore kaa adhyayan kar rahe hai
 Parrikar said, "the second aspect is the commitment to the agreement and the proper information that we have sought
 ham unke jawaab kaa intjaar kar rahe hai
 Let the answer come
 '(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) haalanki raksha mantri ne yah bhi kaha ki vah nausena dwaara unhen di gai jaankaree ke aadhaar par bol rahe hai
 He said that there are certain areas of concern as the Ministry is moving ahead keeping in mind the worst situation
 unhone yah bhi spasht kiya ki scorpine pandubbiyon se sambandhit dastavejon ke li hone se france ke saath kiye ja rahe kisi bhi saude par koi asar nahin padegaa, jinamein rafel ladaaku vimaan sauda bhi shaamil he
 The Defense Minister said that the leaked documents on the web portal of 'the Australian' newspaper did not mention any of Scorpene's weapons system as reported in the media
 parrikar ne kaha ki nausena ne unhen aashwaasan diya he ki adhiktar li hue dastavej chintaa paidaa karne vaale nahin hai
 He said, "arms system agreements are with arms manufacturers and they are separate agreements
 duusari baat ki sabhi pandubbiyon kaa abhi tak samudri pareekshan bhi nahin hua he
 So the most important thing (submarine activity) is not included in the documents
 ' lekin kuch hi ghante baad patrkaar camran stewart ne kaha ki ye chijen bhi li hui hai
 Stewart, in partnership with French company DCNS in Mumbai, published news related to the leaking of over 22,000 pages of highly confidential information relating to the capabilities of six state-of-the-art submarines being built for the Indian Navy
 stewart ne twit kiya, 'bhartiya raksha mantri kaa kahana he ki scorpine pandubbiyon par li hui jaankaree main shastr pranali kii jaankaree shaamil nahin he
 is wrong
 ham hathiyaaron se sambandhit dastavej somvaar ko jari karenge
 He said, "when i am saying that we will release the leaked documents on the Scorpene weapons system, then we will obviously edit sensitive information in it
" ' Sources in the Ministry of Defense also have not paid attention to the leak, saying that it does not compromise with national security, as the documents are out of date and do not contain details of the weapon system
 raksha mantri ne yah bhi kaha ki scorpine panudbbi ne samudri pareekshan tak puraa nahin kiya he jo yah samajhane ke liye mahatvapurn he ki yah pani ke andar kaise kaam karegi
 The Indian Navy has taken up the Scorpene Document Leak Case with the Director General of Arms of France
 parrikar ne raksha website bharatshakti dot in dwaara yojit ek seminar se itar samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'hamen report kaa intjaar he
 Actually the content put on the website is not a big concern
 ham apane aap maan rahe hai ki yah li hui he or ham sabhi ehtiyaat barat rahe hai
 ' parrikar ne kaha, 'jo mujhe bataaya gaya he, uske anusaar yah maanate hue kuch chintaa ke kshetra hai ki jo li hone kaa daawa kiya gaya he, vah vaaki main li hua he
 'they said,' We are considering it the worst case scenario
 lekin mujhe lagata he ki badi chintaa vaali baat nahin he kyonki ham sahi pariprekshya main chizon ko rakhane main safal honge
 When a journalist asked if the leak would affect the Rafale deal, the defense minister retorted and asked if anyone would stop using products from a French company because information was leaked at another company
 parrikar ne kaha ki karrwai nivida main ullikhit sharton par aadhaarit honi chahie
 According to media reports from France, the documents were stolen by a former DCNS employee, while India has not found anything in writing about it
 mumbai main france kii ek company ke saath saajhedaari main bhartiya nausena ke liye banaai jari chah atyaadhunik pandubbiyon kii kshamtaaon se sambandhit atyant gopneey jaankaree ke 22,000 se adhik prishth li ho gaye, jiske baad suraksha mahakama chaukanna ho gaya
 3 by French shipbuilder DCNS at Mazagaon dock
 5 arab dollar kii laagat se banaai ja rahi scorpine pandubbiyon kii ladaaku kshamta se sambandhit jaankaree us samay saarvajanik ho gai jab australian akhbaar ne ise apni website par daal diya
 When the Defense Minister was asked whether DCNS should not have informed India about the leak, which is said to be happening in 2011, Parrikar said the government would wait for an official reply from the company
 tippaniyan He said, 'one aspect is safety which is the first priority for us
 hamane ek team banaai he
 They are studying the details assuming the leaks
 ' parrikar ne kaha, 'doosraa pahalu qaraar sambandhi patibaddhta or uchit soochna kaa he jo hamane maangi he
 We are waiting for their reply
